# 04.10.2019 Database for libretro FBNeo 0.2.97.44 by Krahs
# Based on FinalBurn Neo official arcade dat at https://github.com/libretro/FBNeo/tree/master/dats
# and resolution matching with official MAME 0.214b xml database (mame -listxml).
#
# Name, H pixels, Scanlines, Frame Rate, H position, H zoom, V position,
# H Front Porch, H Sync, H Back Porch, V Sync, H Frequency, Core, Orientation.
#
# Name          :  Name of game(zip) to launch.
# H pixels      :  Horizontal resolution.
# Scanlines     :  Vertical resolution of the game, number of lines of the game.
# Frame Rate    :  Frame Rate of the game in Hz.
#
# H Position    :  Horizontal Position, use this value to move screen horizontally.
# H Zoom        :  Horizontal Zoom, use this value to zoom/unzoom horizontal screen.
# V Position    :  Vertical Position, use this value to move screen vertically.
#
# H Front Porch :  Horizontal Front Porch
# H Sync        :  Horizontal Synchronisation
# H Back Porch  :  Horizontal Back Porch
# V Sync        :  Vertical  Synchronisation
# H Frequency   :  Horizontal Frequency, can be tweaked to force 625 lines mode (e.g. 15840 at 55Hz)
#
# Core          :  Libretro core to use.
# Orientation   :  Game Orientation, can be HORIZONTAL(H) or VERTICAL(V).

# Game H pixels :  Horizontal Resolution of the game.
